------------- 04-03-55-52-308335 Accuracy reward: 0.0 -------------
Content: Given the lengths of the sides D G and A B as well as the lengths of the remaining sides of the triangle, we can use the Law of Cosines to find D C. ------------- 04-04-31-37-869034 Accuracy reward: 0.0 -------------
Content: <Thought>Let's denote the median AD of \triangle ABC as x, AC as y, and BC as z. <br>We know that the median of a triangle divides it into two equal areas.
